    release: v4.3.0 WebUI React+Vite MPA

@@ -1,5 +1,19 @@
 # 更新日志
 
+## [4.3.0] - 2026-03-27
+
+### 变更
+
+- ✨ **WebUI 前端重构为 React + Vite + TypeScript（向后兼容）**
+  - 检测控制台迁移至 `webui/` 工程，构建产物写入 `api/static/`（`webui.html`、共享 `assets/*`）
+  - 摄像头、推理、SSE、参数与 Canvas 叠加与既有 `/api/webui/*` 契约一致
+- ✨ **Vite 多页应用：首页与控制台分离**
+  - `GET /` 优先提供构建后的 `index.html`（`src/landing/`，便于扩展用户界面）；未构建时回退 `api/templates/landing.html`
+  - `GET /webui` 提供 `webui.html`；未构建时返回明确 404 提示
+- Makefile 新增 `webui-dev` / `webui-build`；`AGENTS.md` 与 `webui/README.md` 同步说明
+
+---
+
 ## [4.2.1] - 2026-03-19
 
 ### 变更

-function extractPosePoints(person) {
-  // 兼容格式:
-  // 1) [[x,y,...], ...]
-  // 2) [{x,y,...}, ...]
-  // 3) {keypoints:[...]} / {landmarks:[...]}
-  // 4) {0:[x,y],1:[x,y],...}

-      raw = person.landmark;
-    } else if (Array.isArray(person.landmarks)) {
-      raw = person.landmarks;
-    } else {
-      raw = Object.values(person);
-    }
-  }
-  if (!Array.isArray(raw)) {
-    return [];
-  }
-
-  const points = [];
-  raw.forEach((p) => {
-    if (Array.isArray(p) && p.length >= 2) {
-      const x = Number(p[0]);
-      const y = Number(p[1]);
-      if (Number.isFinite(x) && Number.isFinite(y)) {
-        const score2 = Number(p[2]);
-        const score3 = Number(p[3]);
-        points.push({
-          x,
-          y,
-          visibility: Number.isFinite(score2) ? score2 : (Number.isFinite(score3) ? score3 : null),
-        });
-      }
-      return;
-    }
-    if (p && typeof p === "object") {
-      const x = Number(p.x);
-      const y = Number(p.y);
-      if (Number.isFinite(x) && Number.isFinite(y)) {

-          x,
-          y,
-          visibility: Number.isFinite(Number(p.visibility)) ? Number(p.visibility) : null,
-          index: Number.isFinite(Number(p.index)) ? Number(p.index) : null,
-        });
-      }
-    }
-  });
-  return points;
-}

-function isNormalizedPose(points) {

-function isRenderablePoint(pt) {

-    return false;

-function getContainTransform(canvasW, canvasH, srcW, srcH) {
-  const scale = Math.min(canvasW / Math.max(1, srcW), canvasH / Math.max(1, srcH));
-  const drawW = srcW * scale;
-  const drawH = srcH * scale;
-  const offsetX = (canvasW - drawW) / 2;
-  const offsetY = (canvasH - drawH) / 2;
-  return { scale, offsetX, offsetY };
-}

-function toCanvasPoint(x, y, srcW, srcH, transform, coordinateSpace) {
-  const normalized = coordinateSpace === "frame_normalized";
-  const px = normalized ? x * srcW : x;
-  const py = normalized ? y * srcH : y;
-  return [
-    transform.offsetX + px * transform.scale,
-    transform.offsetY + py * transform.scale,
-  ];
-}

-async function sendFrameForInfer() {

-    return;
-  }

-    const requestId = ++latestRequestId;

-    temp.height = videoEl.videoHeight;
-    temp.getContext("2d").drawImage(videoEl, 0, 0, temp.width, temp.height);

-      temp.toBlob(resolve, "image/jpeg", Number(settings.jpeg_quality || 0.8))
-    );
-    if (!blob) {
-      return;
-    }
-
-    const formData = new FormData();
-    formData.append("file", blob, "frame.jpg");
-
-    const response = await fetch(`/api/webui/infer?threshold=${encodeURIComponent(settings.threshold)}`, {
-      method: "POST",
-      body: formData,
-    });
-    if (!response.ok) {
-      throw new Error(await response.text());
-    }
-    const payload = await response.json();
-    if (requestId !== latestRequestId) {
-      return;
-    }
-
-    latestFrameBitmap = typeof createImageBitmap === "function" ? await createImageBitmap(temp) : temp;
-    updateCameraInfoFromPayload(payload);
-    frameCounter += 1;
-    if (payload.cheating_detected) {
-      detectionCounter += 1;
-    }

-    metricLatency.textContent = Number(payload.detection_time || 0).toFixed(2);

-    lastTick = now;
-    metricFps.textContent = (1000 / dt).toFixed(1);

-    drawPayload(payload);

-    inferInFlight = false;
-  }

 ## 故障排除
 
+### 问题：Windows ARM64 大量依赖安装失败
+
+**现象**：`poetry install` 时 `numpy`、`scipy`、`contourpy`、`httptools` 编译失败（`Could not find vswhere.exe` / `Unknown compiler`），`opencv-python`、`torch`、`torchvision` 报 `Unable to find installation candidates`（wheel 不兼容）。
+
+**原因**：Windows ARM64 的 Python 生态极不成熟——PyTorch、OpenCV 等均未发布 ARM64 wheel，源码编译又需要 Visual Studio C++ 编译器。
+
+**解决方案**：安装 **x86_64（64-bit）版本**的 Python 3.12 或 3.13。Windows ARM 内置 x86_64 仿真层，所有预编译 wheel 均可正常使用，性能约为原生的 70-80%。
+
+```powershell
+# 1) 从 python.org 下载 "Windows installer (64-bit)"（不是 ARM64）
+#    https://www.python.org/downloads/release/python-31310/
+
+# 2) 验证安装的是 x86_64 版本
+py -3.13 -c "import platform; print(platform.machine())"
+# 输出必须是 AMD64（不是 ARM64）
+
+# 3) 安装 Poetry 并重建环境
+py -3.13 -m pip install poetry
+py -3.13 -m poetry env remove --all
+py -3.13 -m poetry install
+py -3.13 -m poetry run python main.py
+```
+
+### 问题：Python 3.14 下 numpy/scipy/torch 编译失败
+
+**现象**：`poetry install` 时 `numpy`、`scipy` 等尝试从源码编译，报 `Unknown compiler` 或 `meson setup` 错误。
+
+**原因**：Python 3.14 发布时间过早，主流科学计算库（numpy、scipy、torch、opencv-python）尚未发布适配 3.14 的预编译 wheel。
+
+**解决方案**：使用 **Python 3.12 或 3.13**（推荐 3.13），所有 wheel 齐全，无需编译。
+
+```powershell
+# Windows
+py -3.13 -m pip install poetry
+py -3.13 -m poetry env remove --all
+py -3.13 -m poetry install
+```
+
+```bash
+# macOS / Linux
+python3.13 -m pip install poetry
+python3.13 -m poetry env remove --all
+python3.13 -m poetry install
+```
+
+### 问题：卸载旧 Python 后 `poetry` 命令报 `Fatal error in launcher`
+
+**现象**：`poetry --version` 报 `Fatal error in launcher: Unable to create process using ...`。
+
+**原因**：Poetry 的 `.exe` launcher 绑定了旧 Python 路径，卸载后找不到解释器。
+
+**解决方案**：用新 Python 重装 Poetry，通过 `py -m poetry` 方式调用绕过旧 launcher。
+
+```powershell
+py -3.13 -m pip install poetry
+py -3.13 -m poetry --version      # 替代 poetry --version
+py -3.13 -m poetry install        # 替代 poetry install
+py -3.13 -m poetry run python main.py
+```
+
+### 问题：UTM / 虚拟机中摄像头不可用
+
+**现象**：WebUI 页面加载正常，但摄像头初始化失败或无画面。
+
+**原因**：UTM 等虚拟化工具的 USB 直通功能有限，无法将物理摄像头直通到虚拟机内。
+
+**解决方案**：
+
+- 推荐直接在**宿主机**（macOS / Windows 物理机）上运行项目
+- 如需在虚拟机内测试，可通过 API（`/docs` Swagger）上传静态图片测试检测功能
+
 ### 问题：程序运行慢
 
 1. 在 `config/config.yaml` 中降低摄像头分辨率

@@ -0,0 +1,29 @@
+# Visual WebUI（React + Vite + TypeScript，多页）
+
+源码位于 `webui/src/`；生产构建产物输出到 `../api/static/`，由 FastAPI 提供：
+
+| 构建产物 | 路由 | 说明 |
+|----------|------|------|
+| `index.html` | `GET /` | 落地页 / 未来用户界面（`src/landing/`） |
+| `webui.html` | `GET /webui` | 检测控制台（原单页应用） |
+| `assets/*` | `/webui/static/assets/*` | 两页共享打包资源 |
+
+未执行构建时，`GET /` 会回退到 `api/templates/landing.html`；`GET /webui` 必须已构建，否则 404。
+
+## 开发
+
+1. 先启动后端（例如 `make api` 或 `uvicorn api.main:app --host 0.0.0.0 --port 8000`）。
+2. 在 `webui/` 执行 `npm install`（首次）与 `npm run dev`。
+3. 浏览器访问：`/` 为落地页，`/webui.html` 为检测面板；`/api` 与 `/webui/outputs` 由 Vite 代理到 `http://127.0.0.1:8000`。
+
+## 生产构建
+
+```bash
+cd webui && npm run build
+```
+
+构建会清空并写入 `api/static/`（`index.html`、`webui.html`、带 hash 的 `assets/*`、`public/` 资源）。部署前需执行此步骤后再启动 API。
+
+## Makefile
+
+仓库根目录提供 `make webui-build`（仅 `npm run build`）与 `make webui-dev`（`npm run dev`）。

+import { Fragment, useRef } from "react";
+import { useVisualWebUI } from "./hooks/useVisualWebUI";
+import { getExportId, normalizeOutputPath, toOutputUrl } from "./lib/exports";
+import type { ExportItem, ExportManifest } from "./types/webui";
+import "./index.css";
+
+function ExportLinks(props: {
+  item: ExportItem;
+  manifest: ExportManifest | { error: string } | undefined;
+  onToggle: (item: ExportItem) => void;
+  expanded: boolean;
+}) {
+  const { item, manifest, expanded, onToggle } = props;
+
+  function createExportLink(
+    label: string,
+    path: string | undefined,
+    options: { download?: boolean } = {},
+  ) {
+    const url = toOutputUrl(path);
+    if (!url) {
+      return null;
+    }
+    const normalized = normalizeOutputPath(path);
+    return (
+      <a
+        className="export-link"
+        href={url}
+        download={options.download ? normalized.split("/").pop() || "" : undefined}
+        target={options.download ? undefined : "_blank"}
+        rel={options.download ? undefined : "noreferrer"}
+      >
+        {label}
+      </a>
+    );
+  }
+
+  const manifestPath = normalizeOutputPath(item.frame_manifest_path);
+  const frames =
+    manifest && "frames" in manifest && Array.isArray(manifest.frames)
+      ? manifest.frames
+      : null;
+
+  return (
+    <li className="export-item">
+      <button
+        type="button"
+        className="export-toggle"
+        onClick={() => {
+          void onToggle(item);
+        }}
+      >
+        <span className="export-caret">{expanded ? "▾" : "▸"}</span>
+        <span className="export-title">
+          {item.event_id || "未知事件"}{" "}
+          {item.timestamp ? `@ ${item.timestamp}` : ""}
+        </span>
+      </button>
+      <div className="export-meta">{item.summary || "无告警摘要"}</div>
+      {expanded ? (
+        <div className="export-details">
+          <div className="export-links">
+            {createExportLink("下载视频", item.clip_path, { download: true })}
+            {createExportLink("打开截图", item.screenshot_path)}
+            {createExportLink("打开清单", item.frame_manifest_path)}
+          </div>
+          {(item.raw_frames_dir || item.frame_manifest_path) ? (
+            <div className="export-meta">
+              {[
+                item.raw_frames_dir ? `原始帧目录: ${item.raw_frames_dir}` : "",
+                item.frame_manifest_path ? `清单路径: ${item.frame_manifest_path}` : "",
+              ]
+                .filter(Boolean)
+                .join(" | ")}
+            </div>
+          ) : null}
+          {manifest && "error" in manifest ? (
+            <div className="export-meta">{manifest.error}</div>
+          ) : null}
+          {frames && frames.length > 0 ? (
+            <>
+              <div className="export-frame-links">
+                {frames.slice(0, 12).map((frame) => (
+                  <Fragment key={`${frame.index}-${frame.file}`}>
+                    {createExportLink(`帧 ${frame.index}`, frame.file)}
+                  </Fragment>
+                ))}
+              </div>
+              {frames.length > 12 ? (
+                <div className="export-meta">
+                  已显示前 12 帧，共 {frames.length}{" "}
+                  帧，可通过“打开清单”查看全部。
+                </div>
+              ) : null}
+            </>
+          ) : null}
+          {manifestPath && !manifest ? (
+            <div className="export-meta">正在加载清单...</div>
+          ) : null}
+        </div>
+      ) : null}
+    </li>
+  );
+}
+
+export default function App() {
+  const videoRef = useRef<HTMLVideoElement>(null);
+  const frameCanvasRef = useRef<HTMLCanvasElement>(null);
+  const overlayCanvasRef = useRef<HTMLCanvasElement>(null);
+  const stageShellRef = useRef<HTMLElement>(null);
+  const stageRef = useRef<HTMLElement>(null);
+
+  const ui = useVisualWebUI({
+    videoRef,
+    frameCanvasRef,
+    overlayCanvasRef,
+    stageShellRef,
+    stageRef,
+  });
+
+  return (
+    <main className="layout">
+      <section ref={stageShellRef} className="stage-shell">
+        <section ref={stageRef} className="stage">
+          <video
+            ref={videoRef}
+            id="camera"
+            autoPlay
+            playsInline
+            muted
+          />
+          <canvas id="frameLayer" ref={frameCanvasRef} />
+          <canvas id="overlay" ref={overlayCanvasRef} />
+          <div id="statusBadge" className={`badge ${ui.badgeMode}`}>
+            {ui.badgeText}
+          </div>
+        </section>
+      </section>
+
+      <aside className="panel">
+        <h1>Visual WebUI</h1>
+        <div className="alerts">
+          <h2>实时告警</h2>
+          <ul id="alertsList">
+            {ui.alerts.length === 0 ? (
+              <li className="empty">暂无告警</li>
+            ) : (
+              ui.alerts.slice(0, 8).map((text, idx) => (
+                <li key={`${idx}-${text}`}>{text}</li>
+              ))
+            )}
+          </ul>
+        </div>
+
+        <div className="actions">
+          <button
+            type="button"
+            id="startBtn"
+            onClick={() => {
+              void ui.startSession().catch((err) => {
+                console.error(err);
+                ui.setBadge("启动失败", "alert");
+              });
+            }}
+          >
+            开始检测
+          </button>
+          <button
+            type="button"
+            id="stopBtn"
+            className="secondary"
+            onClick={() => {
+              void ui.stopSession().catch((err) => {
+                console.error(err);
+                ui.setBadge("停止失败", "alert");
+              });
+            }}
+          >
+            停止检测
+          </button>
+        </div>

+            <span>会话帧数</span>

+            <span>判定阈值</span>
+            <input

+              type="range"
+              min={0}
+              max={1}
+              step={0.01}

+              }}
+            />
+            <strong id="thresholdValue">
+              {Number(ui.settings.threshold).toFixed(2)}
+            </strong>
+          </label>
+          <label className="field">
+            <span>推理间隔(ms)</span>
+            <input
+              id="inferIntervalInput"
+              type="range"
+              min={50}
+              max={1000}
+              step={10}
+              value={ui.settings.infer_interval_ms}
+              onChange={(e) => {
+                ui.updateSettings({ infer_interval_ms: Number(e.target.value) });

+              {String(ui.settings.infer_interval_ms)}

+            <input
+              id="jpegQualityInput"

+              max={1}

+++ b/webui/src/api/webuiClient.ts
@@ -0,0 +1,106 @@
+import type {
+  ExportItem,
+  FrameUIResult,
+  WebUISettings,
+  WebUISettingsRequest,
+} from "../types/webui";
+
+export async function fetchWebUISettings(): Promise<WebUISettings> {
+  const response = await fetch("/api/webui/settings");
+  if (!response.ok) {
+    throw new Error(await response.text());
+  }
+  const data = (await response.json()) as WebUISettings;
+  return data;
+}
+
+export async function postWebUISettings(
+  body: WebUISettingsRequest,
+): Promise<WebUISettings> {
+  const response = await fetch("/api/webui/settings", {
+    method: "POST",
+    headers: { "Content-Type": "application/json" },
+    body: JSON.stringify(body),
+  });
+  if (!response.ok) {
+    throw new Error(await response.text());
+  }
+  const data = (await response.json()) as { settings: WebUISettings };
+  return data.settings;
+}
+
+export async function postWebUIStart(threshold: number): Promise<void> {
+  const response = await fetch("/api/webui/start", {
+    method: "POST",
+    headers: { "Content-Type": "application/json" },
+    body: JSON.stringify({ threshold }),
+  });
+  if (!response.ok) {
+    throw new Error(await response.text());
+  }
+}
+
+export async function postWebUIStop(): Promise<{
+  flush_state?: {
+    event_persisted?: boolean;
+    event_id?: string;
+    event_clip_path?: string;
+    event_raw_frames_path?: string;
+  };
+} | null> {
+  const response = await fetch("/api/webui/stop", { method: "POST" });
+  if (!response.ok) {
+    return null;
+  }
+  return (await response.json()) as {
+    flush_state?: {
+      event_persisted?: boolean;
+      event_id?: string;
+      event_clip_path?: string;
+      event_raw_frames_path?: string;
+    };
+  };
+}
+
+export async function fetchWebUIExports(limit = 8): Promise<ExportItem[]> {
+  const response = await fetch(`/api/webui/exports?limit=${encodeURIComponent(String(limit))}`);
+  if (!response.ok) {
+    throw new Error(await response.text());
+  }
+  const data = (await response.json()) as { items?: ExportItem[] };
+  return Array.isArray(data.items) ? data.items : [];
+}
+
+export async function inferFrame(
+  blob: Blob,
+  threshold: number,
+): Promise<FrameUIResult> {
+  const formData = new FormData();
+  formData.append("file", blob, "frame.jpg");
+  const response = await fetch(
+    `/api/webui/infer?threshold=${encodeURIComponent(String(threshold))}`,
+    {
+      method: "POST",
+      body: formData,
+    },
+  );
+  if (!response.ok) {
+    throw new Error(await response.text());
+  }
+  return (await response.json()) as FrameUIResult;
+}
+
+export function openWebUIStream(
+  onMessage: (data: unknown) => void,
+): EventSource {
+  const stream = new EventSource("/api/webui/stream");
+  stream.onmessage = (event) => {
+    try {
+      const data = JSON.parse(event.data) as unknown;
+      onMessage(data);
+    } catch {
+      /* ignore */
+    }
+  };
+  return stream;
+}

+import {
+  useCallback,
+  useEffect,
+  useLayoutEffect,
+  useRef,
+  useState,
+} from "react";
+import type { RefObject } from "react";
+import {
+  fetchWebUIExports,
+  fetchWebUISettings,
+  inferFrame,
+  openWebUIStream,
+  postWebUISettings,
+  postWebUIStart,
+  postWebUIStop,
+} from "../api/webuiClient";
+import { drawDetectionOverlay, drawFrameSnapshot } from "../lib/draw";
+import { fetchExportManifest, getExportId, normalizeOutputPath } from "../lib/exports";
+import { pushHistoryMessage, type HistoryEntry } from "../lib/history";
+import type {
+  BadgeMode,
+  ExportItem,
+  ExportManifest,
+  FrameUIResult,
+  WebUISettings,
+} from "../types/webui";
+import { defaultWebUISettings } from "../types/webui";
+
+function formatRatio(width: number, height: number): string {
+  if (!width || !height) {
+    return "-";
+  }
+  const value = width / Math.max(1, height);
+  return `${value.toFixed(3)} (${width}:${height})`;
+}
+
+type UseVisualWebUIParams = {
+  videoRef: RefObject<HTMLVideoElement | null>;
+  frameCanvasRef: RefObject<HTMLCanvasElement | null>;
+  overlayCanvasRef: RefObject<HTMLCanvasElement | null>;
+  stageShellRef: RefObject<HTMLElement | null>;
+  stageRef: RefObject<HTMLElement | null>;
+};
+
+export function useVisualWebUI({
+  videoRef,
+  frameCanvasRef,
+  overlayCanvasRef,
+  stageShellRef,
+  stageRef,
+}: UseVisualWebUIParams) {
+  const [settings, setSettings] = useState<WebUISettings>(defaultWebUISettings);
+  const settingsRef = useRef(settings);
+  useLayoutEffect(() => {
+    settingsRef.current = settings;
+  }, [settings]);
+
+  const [running, setRunning] = useState(false);
+  const runningRef = useRef(false);
+  useEffect(() => {
+    runningRef.current = running;
+  }, [running]);
+
+  const [badgeText, setBadgeText] = useState("待启动");
+  const [badgeMode, setBadgeMode] = useState<BadgeMode>("idle");
+  const [alerts, setAlerts] = useState<string[]>([]);
+  const [historyMessages, setHistoryMessages] = useState<HistoryEntry[]>([]);
+  const historyTimesRef = useRef<Map<string, number>>(new Map());
+
+  const [frameCounter, setFrameCounter] = useState(0);
+  const [detectionCounter, setDetectionCounter] = useState(0);
+  const [metricFps, setMetricFps] = useState("-");
+  const [metricLatency, setMetricLatency] = useState("-");
+  const [cameraResolution, setCameraResolution] = useState("-");
+  const [cameraRatio, setCameraRatio] = useState("-");
+  const [stageResolution, setStageResolution] = useState("-");
+  const [stageRatio, setStageRatio] = useState("-");
+
+  const [recentExports, setRecentExports] = useState<ExportItem[]>([]);
+  const [expandedExportIds, setExpandedExportIds] = useState<Set<string>>(
+    () => new Set(),
+  );
+  const expandedExportIdsRef = useRef(expandedExportIds);
+  useEffect(() => {
+    expandedExportIdsRef.current = expandedExportIds;
+  }, [expandedExportIds]);
+
+  const [exportManifestCache, setExportManifestCache] = useState<
+    Map<string, ExportManifest | { error: string }>
+  >(() => new Map());
+  const exportManifestCacheRef = useRef(exportManifestCache);
+  useEffect(() => {
+    exportManifestCacheRef.current = exportManifestCache;
+  }, [exportManifestCache]);
+
+  const [latestPayload, setLatestPayload] = useState<FrameUIResult | null>(null);
+  const latestFrameBitmapRef = useRef<ImageBitmap | HTMLCanvasElement | null>(null);
+
+  const inferInFlightRef = useRef(false);
+  const latestRequestIdRef = useRef(0);
+  const lastTickRef = useRef(performance.now());
+  const lastCheatingDetectedRef = useRef(false);
+  const lastAlertSignatureRef = useRef("");
+  const streamRef = useRef<EventSource | null>(null);
+  const captureTimerRef = useRef<number | null>(null);
+  const cameraTrackRef = useRef<MediaStreamTrack | null>(null);
+  const cameraInfoPollTimerRef = useRef<number | null>(null);
+
+  const appendHistory = useCallback((text: string, options?: { cooldownMs?: number }) => {
+    setHistoryMessages((prev) => {
+      const { messages, times } = pushHistoryMessage(
+        prev,
+        historyTimesRef.current,
+        text,
+        options || {},
+      );
+      historyTimesRef.current = times;
+      return messages;
+    });
+  }, []);
+
+  const setBadge = useCallback((text: string, mode: BadgeMode) => {
+    setBadgeText(text);
+    setBadgeMode(mode);
+  }, []);
+
+  const updateCameraInfo = useCallback(() => {
+    const videoEl = videoRef.current;
+    const stageEl = stageRef.current;
+    if (!videoEl) {
+      return;
+    }
+    const trackSettings =
+      cameraTrackRef.current && typeof cameraTrackRef.current.getSettings === "function"
+        ? cameraTrackRef.current.getSettings()
+        : {};
+    const trackW = Number((trackSettings as { width?: number }).width || 0);
+    const trackH = Number((trackSettings as { height?: number }).height || 0);
+    const vw = videoEl.videoWidth || trackW || 0;
+    const vh = videoEl.videoHeight || trackH || 0;
+    setCameraResolution(vw && vh ? `${vw}x${vh}` : "-");
+    setCameraRatio(formatRatio(vw, vh));
+
+    const sw = Math.round(stageEl?.clientWidth || 0);
+    const sh = Math.round(stageEl?.clientHeight || 0);
+    setStageResolution(sw && sh ? `${sw}x${sh}` : "-");
+    setStageRatio(formatRatio(sw, sh));
+  }, [videoRef, stageRef]);
+
+  const updateCameraInfoFromPayload = useCallback(
+    (payload: FrameUIResult) => {
+      const stageEl = stageRef.current;
+      const overlay = overlayCanvasRef.current;
+      const fw = Number(payload?.frame_size?.width || 0);
+      const fh = Number(payload?.frame_size?.height || 0);
+      if (fw > 0 && fh > 0) {
+        setCameraResolution(`${fw}x${fh}`);
+        setCameraRatio(formatRatio(fw, fh));
+      }
+      const sw = Math.round(stageEl?.clientWidth || overlay?.width || 0);
+      const sh = Math.round(stageEl?.clientHeight || overlay?.height || 0);
+      if (sw > 0 && sh > 0) {
+        setStageResolution(`${sw}x${sh}`);
+        setStageRatio(formatRatio(sw, sh));
+      }
+    },
+    [overlayCanvasRef, stageRef],
+  );
+
+  const redrawCanvases = useCallback(() => {
+    const frameCanvasEl = frameCanvasRef.current;
+    const canvasEl = overlayCanvasRef.current;
+    if (!frameCanvasEl || !canvasEl) {
+      return;
+    }
+    const fctx = frameCanvasEl.getContext("2d");
+    const ctx = canvasEl.getContext("2d");
+    if (!fctx || !ctx) {
+      return;
+    }
+    const w = frameCanvasEl.width;
+    const h = frameCanvasEl.height;
+    drawFrameSnapshot(fctx, latestFrameBitmapRef.current, w, h);
+    if (latestPayload) {
+      drawDetectionOverlay(
+        ctx,
+        latestPayload,
+        settingsRef.current,
+        canvasEl.width,
+        canvasEl.height,
+      );
+    } else {
+      ctx.clearRect(0, 0, canvasEl.width, canvasEl.height);
+    }
+  }, [frameCanvasRef, overlayCanvasRef, latestPayload]);
+
+  const resizeOverlay = useCallback(() => {
+    const videoEl = videoRef.current;
+    const canvasEl = overlayCanvasRef.current;
+    const frameCanvasEl = frameCanvasRef.current;
+    if (!videoEl || !canvasEl || !frameCanvasEl) {
+      return;
+    }
+    const rect = videoEl.getBoundingClientRect();
+    const width = Math.max(1, Math.round(rect.width));
+    const height = Math.max(1, Math.round(rect.height));
+    if (canvasEl.width !== width || canvasEl.height !== height) {
+      canvasEl.width = width;
+      canvasEl.height = height;
+    }
+    if (frameCanvasEl.width !== width || frameCanvasEl.height !== height) {
+      frameCanvasEl.width = width;
+      frameCanvasEl.height = height;
+    }
+    redrawCanvases();
+    updateCameraInfo();
+  }, [
+    overlayCanvasRef,
+    frameCanvasRef,
+    redrawCanvases,
+    videoRef,
+    updateCameraInfo,
+  ]);
+
+  const syncStageSize = useCallback(() => {
+    const stageEl = stageRef.current;
+    const stageShellEl = stageShellRef.current;
+    const videoEl = videoRef.current;
+    if (!stageEl || !stageShellEl || !videoEl?.videoWidth || !videoEl?.videoHeight) {
+      return;
+    }
+    const ratio = videoEl.videoWidth / Math.max(1, videoEl.videoHeight);
+    const availableWidth = Math.max(1, stageShellEl.clientWidth - 40);
+    const availableHeight = Math.max(1, stageShellEl.clientHeight - 40);
+    let width = availableWidth;
+    let height = width / ratio;
+    if (height > availableHeight) {
+      height = availableHeight;
+      width = height * ratio;
+    }
+    stageEl.style.width = `${Math.round(width)}px`;
+    stageEl.style.height = `${Math.round(height)}px`;
+    updateCameraInfo();
+  }, [stageRef, stageShellRef, videoRef, updateCameraInfo]);
+
+  const refreshStageAndInfo = useCallback(() => {
+    syncStageSize();
+    resizeOverlay();
+    updateCameraInfo();
+    redrawCanvases();
+  }, [syncStageSize, resizeOverlay, updateCameraInfo, redrawCanvases]);
+
+  const applyPreviewMode = useCallback(() => {
+    const videoEl = videoRef.current;
+    const frameCanvasEl = frameCanvasRef.current;
+    if (!videoEl || !frameCanvasEl) {
+      return;
+    }
+    const mode = String(settingsRef.current.preview_mode || "analysis");
+    if (mode === "live") {
+      videoEl.style.opacity = "1";
+      frameCanvasEl.style.opacity = "0";
+    } else {
+      videoEl.style.opacity = runningRef.current ? "0" : "1";
+      frameCanvasEl.style.opacity = runningRef.current ? "1" : "0";
+    }
+  }, [frameCanvasRef, videoRef]);
+
+  useEffect(() => {
+    applyPreviewMode();
+  }, [settings.preview_mode, running, applyPreviewMode]);
+
+  const loadRecentExports = useCallback(async () => {
+    const items = await fetchWebUIExports(8);
+    setRecentExports(items);
+    const validIds = new Set(items.map((item) => getExportId(item)));
+    setExpandedExportIds((prev) => {
+      const next = new Set([...prev].filter((id) => validIds.has(id)));
+      return next;
+    });
+  }, []);
+
+  const processPayloadSideEffects = useCallback(
+    (payload: FrameUIResult) => {
+      setAlerts(payload.alerts || []);
+      const alertSignature = (payload.alerts || []).join(" | ");
+
+      if (payload.event_started) {
+        const startedEventId = String(payload.event_id || "").trim();
+        appendHistory(
+          startedEventId
+            ? `检测作弊事件开始: ${startedEventId}`
+            : "检测作弊事件开始",
+        );
+      }
+      if (
+        payload.event_finished ||
+        (!payload.cheating_detected && lastCheatingDetectedRef.current)
+      ) {
+        appendHistory("检测作弊事件结束");
+      }
+      if (alertSignature && alertSignature !== lastAlertSignatureRef.current) {
+        appendHistory(`告警记录: ${alertSignature}`, { cooldownMs: 4000 });
+      }
+      if (payload.event_persisted) {
+        const persistedEventId = String(payload.event_id || "").trim();
+        appendHistory(
+          persistedEventId
+            ? `作弊事件记录已保存: ${persistedEventId}`
+            : "作弊事件记录已保存",
+        );
+        if (payload.event_clip_path) {
+          appendHistory(`事件视频已导出: ${payload.event_clip_path}`);
+        }
+        if (payload.event_raw_frames_path) {
+          appendHistory(`事件原始帧已导出: ${payload.event_raw_frames_path}`);
+        }
+        void loadRecentExports();
+      }
+
+      lastCheatingDetectedRef.current = Boolean(payload.cheating_detected);
+      lastAlertSignatureRef.current = alertSignature;
+
+      if (payload.cheating_detected) {
+        setBadge("检测到可疑行为", "alert");
+      } else if (runningRef.current) {
+        setBadge("检测进行中", "active");
+      }
+    },
+    [appendHistory, loadRecentExports, setBadge],
+  );
+
+  const sendFrameForInfer = useCallback(async () => {
+    const videoEl = videoRef.current;
+    if (
+      !runningRef.current ||
+      !videoEl?.videoWidth ||
+      !videoEl?.videoHeight ||
+      inferInFlightRef.current
+    ) {
+      return;
+    }
+    inferInFlightRef.current = true;
+    try {
+      const requestId = ++latestRequestIdRef.current;
+      const temp = document.createElement("canvas");
+      temp.width = videoEl.videoWidth;
+      temp.height = videoEl.videoHeight;
+      const tctx = temp.getContext("2d");
+      if (!tctx) {
+        return;
+      }
+      tctx.drawImage(videoEl, 0, 0, temp.width, temp.height);
+
+      const blob = await new Promise<Blob | null>((resolve) =>
+        temp.toBlob(resolve, "image/jpeg", Number(settingsRef.current.jpeg_quality || 0.8)),
+      );
+      if (!blob) {
+        return;
+      }
+
+      const payload = await inferFrame(blob, settingsRef.current.threshold);
+      if (requestId !== latestRequestIdRef.current) {
+        return;
+      }
+
+      latestFrameBitmapRef.current =
+        typeof createImageBitmap === "function"
+          ? await createImageBitmap(temp)
+          : temp;
+
+      updateCameraInfoFromPayload(payload);
+      setFrameCounter((c) => c + 1);
+      if (payload.cheating_detected) {
+        setDetectionCounter((c) => c + 1);
+      }
+      setMetricLatency(Number(payload.detection_time || 0).toFixed(2));
+
+      const now = performance.now();
+      const dt = Math.max(1, now - lastTickRef.current);
+      lastTickRef.current = now;
+      setMetricFps((1000 / dt).toFixed(1));
+
+      setLatestPayload(payload);
+      processPayloadSideEffects(payload);
+
+      const frameCanvasEl = frameCanvasRef.current;
+      const canvasEl = overlayCanvasRef.current;
+      if (frameCanvasEl && canvasEl) {
+        const fctx = frameCanvasEl.getContext("2d");
+        const ctx = canvasEl.getContext("2d");
+        if (fctx && ctx) {
+          drawFrameSnapshot(
+            fctx,
+            latestFrameBitmapRef.current,
+            frameCanvasEl.width,
+            frameCanvasEl.height,
+          );
+          drawDetectionOverlay(
+            ctx,
+            payload,
+            settingsRef.current,
+            canvasEl.width,
+            canvasEl.height,
+          );
+        }
+      }
+    } finally {
+      inferInFlightRef.current = false;
+    }
+  }, [
+    frameCanvasRef,
+    overlayCanvasRef,
+    processPayloadSideEffects,
+    updateCameraInfoFromPayload,
+    videoRef,
+  ]);
+
+  const startCaptureLoop = useCallback(() => {
+    if (captureTimerRef.current) {
+      window.clearInterval(captureTimerRef.current);
+    }
+    const interval = Math.max(50, Number(settingsRef.current.infer_interval_ms || 120));
+    captureTimerRef.current = window.setInterval(() => {
+      void sendFrameForInfer().catch((err) => {
+        console.error(err);
+        setBadge("推理请求失败", "alert");
+      });
+    }, interval);
+  }, [sendFrameForInfer, setBadge]);
+
+  const stopCaptureLoop = useCallback(() => {
+    if (captureTimerRef.current) {
+      window.clearInterval(captureTimerRef.current);
+      captureTimerRef.current = null;
+    }
+  }, []);
+
+  const connectSSE = useCallback(() => {
+    if (streamRef.current) {
+      streamRef.current.close();
+    }
+    streamRef.current = openWebUIStream((data) => {
+      if (
+        data &&
+        typeof data === "object" &&
+        (data as { type?: string }).type === "frame_result" &&
+        (data as { payload?: FrameUIResult }).payload
+      ) {
+        const p = (data as { payload: FrameUIResult }).payload;
+        setMetricLatency(Number(p.detection_time || 0).toFixed(2));
+      }
+    });
+  }, []);
+
+  const startSession = useCallback(async () => {
+    if (runningRef.current) {
+      return;
+    }
+    await postWebUIStart(Number(settingsRef.current.threshold));
+    setRunning(true);
+    setFrameCounter(0);
+    setDetectionCounter(0);
+    lastAlertSignatureRef.current = "";
+    historyTimesRef.current = new Map();
+    setAlerts([]);
+    setBadge("检测进行中", "active");
+    appendHistory("检测会话开始");
+    applyPreviewMode();
+    lastTickRef.current = performance.now();
+    lastCheatingDetectedRef.current = false;
+    connectSSE();
+    startCaptureLoop();
+  }, [appendHistory, applyPreviewMode, connectSSE, setBadge, startCaptureLoop]);
+
+  const stopSession = useCallback(async () => {
+    setRunning(false);
+    stopCaptureLoop();
+    if (streamRef.current) {
+      streamRef.current.close();
+      streamRef.current = null;
+    }
+    const stopData = await postWebUIStop();
+    latestFrameBitmapRef.current = null;
+    setLatestPayload(null);
+    const frameCanvasEl = frameCanvasRef.current;
+    const canvasEl = overlayCanvasRef.current;
+    if (frameCanvasEl) {
+      const fctx = frameCanvasEl.getContext("2d");
+      if (fctx) {
+        fctx.clearRect(0, 0, frameCanvasEl.width, frameCanvasEl.height);
+      }
+    }
+    if (canvasEl) {
+      const ctx = canvasEl.getContext("2d");
+      if (ctx) {
+        ctx.clearRect(0, 0, canvasEl.width, canvasEl.height);
+      }
+    }
+    applyPreviewMode();
+    if (lastCheatingDetectedRef.current) {
+      appendHistory("检测作弊事件结束");
+    }
+    lastCheatingDetectedRef.current = false;
+    lastAlertSignatureRef.current = "";
+    const flushState = stopData?.flush_state || {};
+    if (flushState.event_persisted) {
+      appendHistory(
+        flushState.event_id
+          ? `作弊事件记录已保存: ${flushState.event_id}`
+          : "作弊事件记录已保存",
+      );
+      if (flushState.event_clip_path) {
+        appendHistory(`事件视频已导出: ${flushState.event_clip_path}`);
+      }
+      if (flushState.event_raw_frames_path) {
+        appendHistory(`事件原始帧已导出: ${flushState.event_raw_frames_path}`);
+      }
+    }
+    await loadRecentExports();
+    appendHistory("检测会话结束");
+    setBadge("已停止", "idle");
+  }, [
+    appendHistory,
+    applyPreviewMode,
+    frameCanvasRef,
+    loadRecentExports,
+    overlayCanvasRef,
+    setBadge,
+    stopCaptureLoop,
+  ]);
+
+  const saveSettings = useCallback(async () => {
+    const s = settingsRef.current;
+    const updated = await postWebUISettings({
+      threshold: s.threshold,
+      infer_interval_ms: s.infer_interval_ms,
+      jpeg_quality: s.jpeg_quality,
+      preview_mode: s.preview_mode,
+      draw_skeleton: s.draw_skeleton,
+      draw_person_bbox: s.draw_person_bbox,
+      draw_suspicious_regions: s.draw_suspicious_regions,
+      draw_point_index: s.draw_point_index,
+      head_only_pose: s.head_only_pose,
+      draw_pose_label: s.draw_pose_label,
+      export_event_video: s.export_event_video,
+      export_raw_frames: s.export_raw_frames,
+    });
+    setSettings({ ...settingsRef.current, ...updated });
+    applyPreviewMode();
+    appendHistory("参数调整保存完成");
+    if (runningRef.current) {
+      startCaptureLoop();
+    }
+    await loadRecentExports();
+  }, [appendHistory, applyPreviewMode, loadRecentExports, startCaptureLoop]);
+
+  const initCamera = useCallback(async () => {
+    const media = await navigator.mediaDevices.getUserMedia({
+      video: { width: 1280, height: 720, facingMode: "user" },
+      audio: false,
+    });
+    cameraTrackRef.current = media.getVideoTracks()[0] || null;
+    const videoEl = videoRef.current;
+    if (!videoEl) {
+      return;
+    }
+    videoEl.srcObject = media;
+    const onMeta = () => {
+      refreshStageAndInfo();
+    };
+    videoEl.addEventListener("loadedmetadata", onMeta);
+    videoEl.addEventListener("resize", onMeta);
+    await videoEl.play();
+    refreshStageAndInfo();
+    if (cameraInfoPollTimerRef.current) {
+      window.clearInterval(cameraInfoPollTimerRef.current);
+    }
+    cameraInfoPollTimerRef.current = window.setInterval(() => {
+      refreshStageAndInfo();
+      if (
+        (videoEl.videoWidth && videoEl.videoHeight) ||
+        (cameraTrackRef.current && cameraTrackRef.current.readyState === "live")
+      ) {
+        const sw = Math.round(stageRef.current?.clientWidth || 0);
+        const sh = Math.round(stageRef.current?.clientHeight || 0);
+        if (sw > 0 && sh > 0 && cameraInfoPollTimerRef.current) {
+          window.clearInterval(cameraInfoPollTimerRef.current);
+          cameraInfoPollTimerRef.current = null;
+        }
+      }
+    }, 300);
+  }, [refreshStageAndInfo, stageRef, videoRef]);
+
+  useEffect(() => {
+    let cancelled = false;
+    void Promise.all([
+      fetchWebUISettings().then((data) => {
+        if (!cancelled) {
+          setSettings({ ...defaultWebUISettings, ...data });
+        }
+      }),
+      loadRecentExports(),
+      initCamera(),
+    ])
+      .then(() => {
+        if (!cancelled) {
+          applyPreviewMode();
+          setBadge("摄像头已就绪", "idle");
+          setAlerts([]);
+          appendHistory("摄像头已就绪，开始接收画面");
+        }
+      })
+      .catch((err) => {
+        console.error(err);
+        if (!cancelled) {
+          setBadge("初始化失败", "alert");
+        }
+      });
+    return () => {
+      cancelled = true;
+    };
+    // 仅挂载时初始化摄像头与设置
+    // eslint-disable-next-line react-hooks/exhaustive-deps
+  }, []);
+
+  useEffect(() => {
+    const onResize = () => {
+      refreshStageAndInfo();
+    };
+    window.addEventListener("resize", onResize);
+    return () => window.removeEventListener("resize", onResize);
+  }, [refreshStageAndInfo]);
+
+  const updateSettings = useCallback((patch: Partial<WebUISettings>) => {
+    setSettings((prev) => ({ ...prev, ...patch }));
+  }, []);
+
+  const toggleExportDetails = useCallback(async (item: ExportItem) => {
+    const exportId = getExportId(item);
+    if (!exportId) {
+      return;
+    }
+    if (expandedExportIdsRef.current.has(exportId)) {
+      setExpandedExportIds((prev) => {
+        const next = new Set(prev);
+        next.delete(exportId);
+        return next;
+      });
+      return;
+    }
+    setExpandedExportIds((prev) => {
+      const next = new Set(prev);
+      next.add(exportId);
+      return next;
+    });
+    const manifestPath = normalizeOutputPath(item.frame_manifest_path);
+    if (!manifestPath || exportManifestCacheRef.current.has(manifestPath)) {
+      return;
+    }
+    try {
+      const data = await fetchExportManifest(manifestPath);
+      setExportManifestCache((prev) => {
+        const next = new Map(prev);
+        next.set(manifestPath, data);
+        return next;
+      });
+    } catch (err) {
+      console.error(err);
+      setExportManifestCache((prev) => {
+        const next = new Map(prev);
+        next.set(manifestPath, { error: "清单加载失败" });
+        return next;
+      });
+    }
+  }, []);
+
+  const redrawOverlayFromLatest = useCallback(() => {
+    if (!latestPayload) {
+      return;
+    }
+    const canvasEl = overlayCanvasRef.current;
+    if (!canvasEl) {
+      return;
+    }
+    const ctx = canvasEl.getContext("2d");
+    if (!ctx) {
+      return;
+    }
+    drawDetectionOverlay(
+      ctx,
+      latestPayload,
+      settingsRef.current,
+      canvasEl.width,
+      canvasEl.height,
+    );
+  }, [latestPayload, overlayCanvasRef]);
+
+  return {
+    settings,
+    updateSettings,
+    running,
+    startSession,
+    stopSession,
+    saveSettings,
+    badgeText,
+    badgeMode,
+    alerts,
+    historyMessages,
+    frameCounter,
+    detectionCounter,
+    metricFps,
+    metricLatency,
+    cameraResolution,
+    cameraRatio,
+    stageResolution,
+    stageRatio,
+    recentExports,
+    expandedExportIds,
+    exportManifestCache,
+    toggleExportDetails,
+    redrawOverlayFromLatest,
+    appendHistory,
+    setBadge,
+  };
+}

+function readVersion(): string {
+  const meta = document.querySelector('meta[name="app-version"]');
+  const raw = meta?.getAttribute("content")?.trim();
+  if (raw && raw !== "__APP_VERSION__") {
+    return raw;
+  }
+  return "dev";
+}
+
+export function LandingApp() {
+  const version = readVersion();
+
+  return (
+    <div className="landing">
+      <h1>监考作弊检测系统</h1>
+      <p className="landing-ver">版本 {version}</p>
+      <p className="landing-lead">
+        基于 OpenCV 与 YOLO 的考场行为检测：摄像头采集、实时推理、可疑事件与证据导出（截图/片段等）。
+      </p>
+      <ul className="landing-list">
+        <li>REST API 与 OpenAPI 交互式文档</li>

+export type PreviewMode = "analysis" | "live";
+
+export type WebUISettings = {
+  threshold: number;
+  infer_interval_ms: number;
+  jpeg_quality: number;
+  draw_skeleton: boolean;
+  draw_person_bbox: boolean;
+  draw_suspicious_regions: boolean;
+  draw_point_index: boolean;
+  head_only_pose: boolean;
+  draw_pose_label: boolean;
+  preview_mode: PreviewMode;
+  export_event_video: boolean;
+  export_raw_frames: boolean;
+};
+
+export type FrameUIResult = {
+  timestamp: string;
+  frame_index: number;
+  frame_size: { width?: number; height?: number };
+  cheating_detected: boolean;
+  alerts: string[];
+  fusion_score: number;
+  detection_time: number;
+  max_alert_level?: string | null;
+  classified_alerts: Array<Record<string, unknown>>;
+  person_bboxes: number[][];
+  suspicious_regions: Array<{
+    bbox: number[];
+    type?: string;
+    confidence?: number;
+  }>;
+  pose_landmarks: unknown[];
+  pose_people: Array<Record<string, unknown>>;
+  fsm_results: Record<string, unknown>;
+  performance: Record<string, unknown>;
+  event_started?: boolean;
+  event_finished?: boolean;
+  event_holding?: boolean;
+  event_persisted?: boolean;
+  event_id?: string | null;
+  event_clip_path?: string | null;
+  event_raw_frames_path?: string | null;
+};
+
+export type WebUISettingsRequest = Partial<WebUISettings>;
+
+export type ExportItem = {
+  event_id?: string;
+  timestamp?: string;
+  summary?: string;
+  clip_path?: string;
+  screenshot_path?: string;
+  frame_manifest_path?: string;
+  raw_frames_dir?: string;
+};
+
+export type ExportManifest = {
+  frames?: Array<{ index: number; file: string }>;
+  error?: string;
+};
+
+export type BadgeMode = "idle" | "active" | "alert";
+
+export const defaultWebUISettings: WebUISettings = {
+  threshold: 0.6,
+  infer_interval_ms: 120,
+  jpeg_quality: 0.8,
+  draw_skeleton: true,
+  draw_person_bbox: true,
+  draw_suspicious_regions: true,
+  draw_point_index: false,
+  head_only_pose: false,
+  draw_pose_label: true,
+  preview_mode: "analysis",
+  export_event_video: true,
+  export_raw_frames: true,
+};

diff --git a/webui/vite.config.ts b/webui/vite.config.ts
new file mode 100644
index 0000000..8c2b91c
--- /dev/null
+++ b/webui/vite.config.ts
@@ -0,0 +1,27 @@
+import { dirname, resolve } from "node:path";
+import { fileURLToPath } from "node:url";
+import { defineConfig } from "vite";
+import react from "@vitejs/plugin-react";
+
+const __dirname = dirname(fileURLToPath(import.meta.url));
+
+export default defineConfig(({ mode }) => ({
+  plugins: [react()],
+  base: mode === "production" ? "/webui/static/" : "/",
+  build: {
+    outDir: "../api/static",
+    emptyOutDir: true,
+    rollupOptions: {
+      input: {
+        index: resolve(__dirname, "index.html"),
+        webui: resolve(__dirname, "webui.html"),
+      },
+    },
+  },
+  server: {
+    proxy: {
+      "/api": { target: "http://127.0.0.1:8000", changeOrigin: true },
+      "/webui/outputs": { target: "http://127.0.0.1:8000", changeOrigin: true },
+    },
+  },
+}));
